</p>
<ol><li>to join</li>
<li>to become familiar <i>(with)</i>, to familiarize oneself <i>(with)</i>, to learn to use, to enjoy

<li>to communicate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщать.html>приобща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priobščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщение.html>приобще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priobščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщение.html>приобще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщение.html>приобще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщение.html>приобще́ний</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-общи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-obščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priobščítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщать.html>приобща́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́ссы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:культура.html>культу́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priobščítʹ</b> širókije mássy k kulʹtúre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give the masses access to (modern) culture</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to join <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priobščítʹ</b> k délu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to file</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">church</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to administer the sacrament <i>(to)</i>, to communicate</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приобщиться.html>приобщи́ться</a> (22976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priobščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщиться.html>приобщи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priobščítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщаться.html>приобща́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to join</li>
<li>to become familiar <i>(with)</i>, to familiarize oneself <i>(with)</i>, to learn to use, to enjoy</li>
<li>to communicate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобщить.html>приобщи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priobščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***припадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a> (13728)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">припа́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pripád-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припасть.html>припа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall down <i>(to)</i>, to press oneself <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грудь.html>груди</a> кого́-л</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripadátʹ</b> k grudi kovó-l</i> ― <span class="e-translation">press oneself against smb's breast</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> чьи́м-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripadátʹ</b> k čʹím-libo nogám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">prostrate oneself before smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripadátʹ</b> úxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">press one's ear (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to limp <i>(slightly)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:припадать.html>припада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вую</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:левый.html>ле́вую</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pripadátʹ</b> na právuju (lévuju) nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be lame in the right (left) leg</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:па.html>па́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>доч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>припа́дочнее, припа́дочней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-припадоч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>Deverbal noun from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припасти.html>припасти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pripastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripás</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́сов</a></b>)

***припасти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припасти.html>припасти́</a> (15860)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припасти.html>припасти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">припаса́ть</b>)

***припев.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́в</a> (25006)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripév</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припев.html>припе́вов</a></b>)
</p>

***припекать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припекать.html>припека́ть</a> (18630)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">припек-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pripek-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припекать.html>припека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">припе́чь</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roast with fire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to harass, to offend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be very hot <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the sun, fire, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнце</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:припекать.html>припека́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sólnce <b>pripekájet</b> sevódnja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sun is beating down today</span></div></dd>
